1. Custom Drop Down

The HTML Structure, Styling and the Scripts that needs to be included are given below

  • HTML
  • Styling
  • Script
  • Result




<div class="custom-dropdown">
<div class="custom-dd-selected">2015</div>
  <div class="custom-dd-list">
    <ul>
      <li class="" data-val="">All</li>
      <li data-val="year_2018">2018</li>
      <li data-val="year_2017">2017</li>
      <li data-val="year_2016">2016</li>
      <li data-val="year_2015">2015</li>
      <li data-val="year_2014">2014</li>
      <li data-val="year_2013">2013</li>
    </ul>
  </div>
</div>






.custom-dropdown {
  background: #fff url("https://thumb.ibb.co/m6mBn7/drop_down_arrow.png") no-repeat 
              94% 20px/ auto;
  border: 1px solid #cccccc;
  border-radius: 3px;
  padding: 10px;
  cursor: pointer;
  position: relative;
  width: 250px;
}
.custom-dd-selected {
  color: #000;
  font: 600 16px/120% "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif;
}
.custom-dropdown .custom-dd-list {
  width: 100%;
  background: #fff;
  display: none;
  border: 1px solid #cccccc;
  border-radius: 3px;
  left: 0;
  position: absolute;
  top: 37px;
  overflow-y: auto;
  z-index: 99;
}
.custom-dd-list ul {
  margin: 0;
  padding: 0;
}
.custom-dd-list ul li {
  font: 600 16px/120% "Source Sans Pro", sans-serif;
  border-bottom: 1px solid #b2b2b2;
  padding: 10px;
  margin: 0;
  list-style-type: none;
}
.custom-dd-list ul li.cdd-active,
.custom-dd-list ul li:hover,
.custom-dd-list ul li:hover a {
  background: #ce2b2b;
  color: #fff;
}






$(".custom-dropdown").click(function() {
var dis = $(this),
  disList = dis.find(".custom-dd-list");
dis.toggleClass("active");
$(".custom-dropdown").not(dis).removeClass("active").find(".custom-dd-list").hide();
disList.toggle();
}).change(function() {
var selectedVal = $(this).find(".custom-dd-list li.cdd-active").data("val")
});
$(".custom-dropdown").find(".custom-dd-list ul li").click(function() {
var dis = $(this),
  parent = dis.parents(".custom-dropdown"),
  selVal = dis.attr("data-val"),
  selHtml = dis.text();
dis.siblings().removeClass("cdd-active");
(typeof selVal != "undefined") && (parent.find(".custom-dd-selected").html(selHtml));
if ((selVal != "") && (typeof selVal != "undefined")) {
  dis.addClass("cdd-active");
  dis.removeClass("active").find(".custom-dd-list").hide();
}
parent.trigger("change");
});
$(document).click(function(e) {
var dis = $(e.target);
if (!dis.hasClass("custom-dropdown") && dis.parents(".custom-dropdown").length <= 0) {
  $(".custom-dropdown").removeClass("active").find(".custom-dd-list").hide();
}
})

body {
  text-align: center;
  padding: 50px 0;
}
#paging {
  margin: 0 auto;
  display: inline-block;
}
#content .each-content {
  width: 80px;
  height: 50px;
  padding: 30px;
  display: inline-block;
  vertical-align: top;
  background: #02ccba;
  color: #fff;
  margin-right: 10px;
  margin-bottom: 50px;
  position: relative;
}
#content .each-content p {
  position: absolute;
  left: 50%;
  top: 50%;
  transform: translate(-50%, -50%);
  margin: 0;
  font-size: 26px;
  font-weight: bold;
}






function initPagination(itemSelector) {
  var perPage = 3;
  $("#content .each-content").removeClass(function(index, css) {
    return (css.match(/(^|\s)page-\S+/g) || []).join(' ');
  });
  $(itemSelector).addClass(function(key, val) {
    return "page-" + (Math.floor(key / perPage) + 1);
  })
  $("#paging")
    .pagination('destroy')
    .pagination({           
      items: $(itemSelector).length,
      itemsOnPage: perPage,
      cssStyle: 'light-theme',
      onPageClick: function(pgno, e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $(itemSelector).hide(0).filter(".page-" + pgno).show(0)
      },
      onInit: function() {
        $(itemSelector).hide(0).filter(".page-1").show(0)
      }
  });
}
initPagination("#content .each-content");
paginationmodule

      <label for="company">Company *</label>
      <input autoComplete="company-name" name="company-name" type="text" value="" data-sfv-minlength="5"

    </div>

    </div>

    <select autoComplete="country-name" name="dropdown" data-sfv-required="yes">

      <option autoComplete="country-name" value="India">India</option>
      <option autoComplete="country-name" value="USA">USA</option>
    </select>
    <button class="btn" type="submit">Submit</button>
  </form>
</div>

function initPagination(itemSelector) {
  var perPage = 3;
  $("#content .each-content").removeClass(function(index, css) {
    return (css.match(/(^|\s)page-\S+/g) || []).join(' ');
  });
  $(itemSelector).addClass(function(key, val) {
    return "page-" + (Math.floor(key / perPage) + 1);
  })
  $("#paging")
    .pagination('destroy')
    .pagination({           
      items: $(itemSelector).length,
      itemsOnPage: perPage,
      cssStyle: 'light-theme',
      onPageClick: function(pgno, e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $(itemSelector).hide(0).filter(".page-" + pgno).show(0)
      },
      onInit: function() {
        $(itemSelector).hide(0).filter(".page-1").show(0)
      }
  });
}
initPagination("#content .each-content");

$(".smooth-scroll").click(function() {
  var dis = $(this),
      target = dis.data("href"),
      offset = parseInt($(target).offset().top),
      header = $(".menu-wrapper");
  dis.addClass("active").siblings().removeClass("active");
  var newOffset = ($(window).width() > 1024) ? offset - (header.outerHeight()) : offset;
  $('html,body').stop().animate({ scrollTop: newOffset }, 200);
});

function findActiveSection() {
  var winHO = $(window).height(),
      winH = winHO - 200;
  return $(".section").map(function() {
    var dis = $(this),
        disY = dis[0].getBoundingClientRect().top;
    if ((disY < winH) && (disY > -200))
      return dis;
    else if ((disY < winHO) && (disY > -200))
      return dis;
  });
}
var prop_scrol_time = "";
if ($(window).width() > 1024) {
  $(window).scroll(function() {
    clearTimeout(prop_scrol_time);
    prop_scrol_time = setTimeout(function() {
      var cActive = findActiveSection();
      $(".smooth-scroll").removeClass("active").filter("[data-href='#" + $(cActive[0]).attr("id") + "']").addClass("active");
    }, 200);
  })
}
smoothscroll

$(document).ready(function() {
  $(".hidden-box").slice(0, 3).show();
  $(".button").on('click', function(){
    $(".hidden-box:hidden").slice(0, 3).slideDown();
  });
});

$(window).load(function(){
  $('.portfolio-item').isotope({
    itemSelector:'.item',
    layoutMode: 'fitRows'
  });
  $('.portfolio-menu ul li').click(function(){
    $('.portfolio-menu ul li').removeClass('active');
    $(this).addClass('active');    
    var selector = $(this).attr('data-filter');
    $('.portfolio-item').isotope({
      filter: selector
    });
    return false;
  });
});

$('.tabgroup > div').hide();
$('.tabgroup > div:first-of-type').show();
$('.tabs a').click(function(e) {
  e.preventDefault();
  var $this = $(this),
    tabgroup = '#' + $this.parents('.tabs').data('tabgroup'),
    others = $this.closest('li').siblings().children('a'),
    target = $this.attr('href');
  others.removeClass('active');
  $this.addClass('active');
  $(tabgroup).children('div').hide();
  $(target).show();
})

  • Script
  • Result




<div class="image-wrap">
  <img src="data:image/png;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAD/ACwAAAAAAQABAAACADs=" data-src="your-image-here">
</div>






function init() {
var imgDefer = document.getElementsByTagName('img');
for (var i=0;i < imgDefer.length; i++) {
if(imgDefer[i].getAttribute('data-src')) {
imgDefer[i].setAttribute('src',imgDefer[i].getAttribute('data-src'));
} } }
window.onload = init;

10. Detecting Devices and Desktop

The HTML Structure, Styling and the Scripts that needs to be included are given below

  • Script




(function($) {
  $(document).ready(function() {
    function isDevice() {
      return /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
    }
    function isDesktop() { return ($(window).width() > 1200) }
    function isMobile() { return ($(window).width() < 768) }
    function isTablet() { return ($(window).width() >= 768 && $(window).width() <= 1024) }
    function isOddRes() { return ($(window).width() > 1024 && $(window).width() <= 1200) }
    function isIpadPro() { return isDevice() && ($(window).width() >= 1366) }
    function isRealDevice() {
      return /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|macintosh|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent) && (typeof(window.orientation) != "undefined" || (navigator.maxTouchPoints > 1));
    }
    function initMview() {
      $("body").addClass("mobileview",isDevice());
    }
    function init() { 
      initMview();
    }
    init();
    var prop_resize_time = "",
        wRevent = isRealDevice() ? "orientationchange" : "resize";
    $(window).on(wRevent,function() {
      clearTimeout(prop_resize_time);
      prop_resize_time = setTimeout(init,200); // Use function which you init  
    });
  })
})(jQuery);
detectingdevicesdesktop

var cookie_policy = Cookies.get('website_cp');
if (cookie_policy == "" || typeof(cookie_policy) == "undefined") {
  $("body").addClass("cookie-bar-active");
}
$("a.closecbar").click(function(e) {
  e.preventDefault();
  Cookies.set('website_cp', 'true');
  $("body").removeClass("cookie-bar-active");
})

$(window).scroll(function() {
var scroll = $(window).scrollTop();
  $(".scroll-to-top").toggleClass("active",(scroll >= 300));
});
$('.to-header').click(function() {
  $('body,html').animate({
    scrollTop: 0
  }, 800);
  return false;
});

$("#list-search").on("input",function() {
  var searchText = $(this).val().trim().toLowerCase().replace(/[ ,.]/g,"");
  if(searchText.length > 1) {
    $(".each-list ul li").hide().removeClass("match").filter(function() {
      return $(this).text().toLowerCase().replace(/[ ,.]/g,"").indexOf(searchText) > -1
    }).show().addClass("match");
    $(".each-list").hide().filter(function() {
      return $(this).find("li.match").length > 0;
    }).show();
    $("#noResult").toggle($(".each-list:visible").length <= 0);
  } else {
    $(".each-list ul li,.each-list").show();
  }
})

 $(".custom-dropdown").click(function() {
  var dis = $(this),
    disList = dis.find(".custom-dd-list");
  dis.toggleClass("active").siblings().removeClass("active").find(".custom-dd-list").hide();
  $(".custom-dropdown").hasClass("active") ? disList.show() : disList.hide();
});
$(".custom-dropdown").change(function() {
  var dis = $(this),
    disVal = dis.find(".custom-dd-list ul li.cdd-active").attr("data-val");
  if (disVal != "" && typeof(disVal) != "undefined") {
    if (dis.hasClass("filter-clients")) {
      filter = disVal == "all" ? "*" : "." + disVal;
      console.log("filter => "+filter);
      ($("#Filter .each-box."+disVal).size() <= 0 && disVal != "all") ? $("#Filter-NoResult").show(): $("#Filter-NoResult").hide();
      $("#Filter .each-box").hide(0);
      initPagination("" + filter + ".each-box");
    }
  } 
});
$(".custom-dropdown").find(".custom-dd-list ul li").click(function() {
  var dis = $(this),
    selVal = dis.attr("data-val"),
    selHtml = dis.text();
  dis.siblings().removeClass("cdd-active");
  if (typeof selVal != "undefined")
    dis.parents(".custom-dropdown").find(".custom-dd-selected").html(selHtml);
  if ((selVal != "") && (typeof selVal != "undefined")) {
    dis.addClass("cdd-active");
    dis.removeClass("active").find(".custom-dd-list").hide();
  }
  dis.parents(".custom-dropdown").trigger("change");
});
//document click
$(document).click(function(e) {
  var dis = $(e.target);
  //close custom dropdown
  if (!dis.hasClass("custom-dropdown") && !dis.parents(".custom-dropdown").hasClass("custom-dropdown")) {
    $(".custom-dropdown").removeClass("active").find(".custom-dd-list").hide();
  }
});
// Pagination
function toggleTitle() {
  $(".publication-wrapper").each(function() {
    $(this).find("h3").toggle(($(this).find(".publication-lists:visible").length > 0))
  })
}
function initPagination(itemSelector) {
  console.log(itemSelector);
  var perPage = 4;
  $("#Filter .each-box").removeClass(function(index, css) {
      return (css.match(/(^|\s)page-\S+/g) || []).join(' ');
  });
  $(itemSelector).addClass(function(key, val) {
      return "page-" + (Math.floor(key / perPage) + 1);
  })
  $("#pagination")
    .pagination('destroy')
    .pagination({
        items: $(itemSelector).length,
        itemsOnPage: perPage,
        cssStyle: 'light-theme',
        onPageClick: function(pgno, e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            $(itemSelector).hide(0).filter(".page-" + pgno).show(0,toggleTitle)
        },
        onInit: function() {
            $(itemSelector).hide(0).filter(".page-1").show(0,toggleTitle)
        }
    });
}
initPagination("#Filter .each-box");

$('.counter').each(function() {
  var $this = $(this),
      countTo = $this.attr('data-count');
  $({ countNum: $this.text()}).animate({
    countNum: countTo
  },
  {
    duration: 8000,
    easing:'linear',
    step: function() {
      $this.text(Math.floor(this.countNum));
    },
    complete: function() {
      $this.text(this.countNum);
    }
  });   
});

$(".filter-clients li").not($(".nofilter")).click(function() {
  var disVal = $(this).data("val"),
      fC = (disVal == "*") ? disVal : "."+disVal;
  $(this).addClass("active").siblings("li").removeClass("active");
  $(".each-box-wrapper .each-box").hide().filter(fC).show();
}).eq(0).trigger("click");
  $('#InnerBodyWrpapper .portfolio-header-wrap ul li').click(function() {
     var offset = $('#InnerBodyWrpapper .each-box-wrapper').offset().top - $("#Header").outerHeight() - 100;
     $('html,body').stop().animate({ scrollTop: offset }, 0);
  });

$(".filter-clients li").not($(".nofilter")).click(function() {
  var disVal = $(this).data("val"),
      fC = (disVal == "*") ? disVal : "."+disVal;
  $(this).addClass("active").siblings("li").removeClass("active");
  $(".each-box-wrapper .each-box").hide().filter(fC).show();
}).eq(0).trigger("click");
  $('#InnerBodyWrpapper .portfolio-header-wrap ul li').click(function() {
     var offset = $('#InnerBodyWrpapper .each-box-wrapper').offset().top - $("#Header").outerHeight() - 100;
     $('html,body').stop().animate({ scrollTop: offset }, 0);
  });

var sclGallery = "",
sclGalCount = 5;
function sgLoadMore() {
  $('.photo-gallery-wrapper .each-gallery-img').hide().filter(function() {
    return ($(this).index() < sclGalCount)
  }).show();
  (sclGallery != "") && (sclGallery.masonry('layout'));
  $(".load-more-cta a").toggle(sclGalCount < $('.photo-gallery-wrapper .each-gallery-img').length)
  sclGalCount += 5;
}
function masonryLayout() {
  (sclGallery != "") && (sclGallery.masonry('destroy'));
  sclGallery = $('.photo-gallery-wrapper').masonry({
    itemSelector: '.each-gallery-img',
    gutter: 5
  });
  sgLoadMore();
}
masonryLayout();
$(".load-more-cta a").click(sgLoadMore);

function findActiveSection() {
  var winHO = $(window).height(),
    adjustVal = 200;
  winH = winHO - adjustVal;
  var $return = $(".board-card").filter(function() {
    return $(this).isInViewport();
  });
  if ($return.length <= 0) {
    $return = $(".board-card:first,.board-card:last").filter(function() {
      return $(this).isInViewport(0);
    });
  }
  return $return;
}

 $(".vertical-tab .each-tab").on("click", function(e) {
    var dis = $(this),
      dataTarget = dis.data("target");
    dis.addClass("active").siblings(".each-tab").removeClass("active");
    $(".vertical-tab-wrapper .vertical-tab-content").hide();
    $(dataTarget).show().addClass("active").siblings().removeClass("active");
});

 $(".lhs-sticky-menu ul").stick_in_parent({
        parent : $(".advisory-boards"), 
        offset_top: $("#Header").outerHeight()
      }); 
       $(".smooth-scroll").click(function() {
      var dis = $(this),
          disTarget = dis.data("target"),
          header = $("#Header"),
          // hval = (header.css('position') == "absolute") ? 0 : $("#Header").outerHeight(),
          scrollTo = parseInt($(disTarget).offset().top); //- hval;
      $('html,body').stop().animate({ scrollTop: scrollTo }, 1000);
      dis.addClass("active").siblings().removeClass("active");
    });
    $.fn.isInViewport = function(opt) {
      opt = typeof(opt) == "undefined" ? 4 : Number(opt);
      var dis = $(this),
          disY = dis[0].getBoundingClientRect().top,
          disH = dis.outerHeight();
          adjustVal = opt > 0 ? (disH / opt) : 0;
      return ((disY < winH) && (Math.abs(disY) < (disH - adjustVal)))
    };
    function findActiveSection() {
      var winHO = $(window).height(),
          adjustVal = 200;
          winH  = winHO - adjustVal;
      var $return = $(".board-card").filter(function() {
        return $(this).isInViewport();
      });
      if($return.length <= 0) {
        $return = $(".board-card:first,.board-card:last").filter(function() {
          return $(this).isInViewport(0);
        });
      }
      return $return;
    }
     var prop_scrol_time = "";
    if ($(window).width() > 1024) {
      $(window).scroll(function() {
        clearTimeout(prop_scrol_time);
        prop_scrol_time = setTimeout(function() {
          var cActive = findActiveSection();
           $(".smooth-scroll").removeClass("active").filter("[data-target='#" + $(cActive[0]).attr("id") + "']").addClass("active");
            }, 200);
      })
    }

 setInterval(function() {
    var target = $(".each-tab"),
        currentActive = target.filter(".active"),
        nextActive = currentActive.next();
    nextActive = nextActive.length > 0 ? nextActive : target.eq(0);
    // nextActive.trigger("click");
nextActive.addClass("active").siblings().removeClass("active");
  },3000)

The point of using Lorem Ipsum is that it has a more-or-less normal distribution of letters, as opposed to using 'Content here, content here', making it look like readable English. Many desktop publishing packages and web page editors now use Lorem Ipsum as their default model text, and a search for 'lorem ipsum' will uncover many web sites still in their infancy. Various versions have evolved over the years, sometimes by accident, sometimes on purpose (injected humour and the like).</p>

Richard McClintock, a Latin professor at Hampden-Sydney College in Virginia, looked up one of the more obscure Latin words, consectetur, from a Lorem Ipsum passage, and going through the cites of the word in classical literature, discovered the undoubtable source. Lorem Ipsum comes from sections 1.10.32 and 1.10.33 of "de Finibus Bonorum et Malorum" (The Extremes of Good and Evil) by Cicero, written in 45 BC. This book is a treatise on the theory of ethics, very popular during the Renaissance. The first line of Lorem Ipsum, "Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet..", comes from a line in section 1.10.32.</p>
      </div>

 $(".tabs-menu a").click(function(event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    $(this).parent().addClass("current");
    $(this).parent().siblings().removeClass("current");
    var tab = $(this).attr("href");
    $(".tab-content").not(tab).css("display", "none");
    $(tab).fadeIn();
  });

 var filterUl = $("<ul/>");
  $("<li/>", {
    "html": "ALL <span class='count_pp'>" + $(".alpha-filter").length + "</span>",
    "data-filter": "*"
  }).appendTo(filterUl);
  for (var i = 65; i <= 90; i++) {
    var alphachar = String.fromCharCode(i),
      charAppered = $(".alpha-filter").filter(function() {
        return $(this).text().trim().charAt(0).toLowerCase() == alphachar.toLowerCase()
      }).get();
    $("<li/>", {
      "html": alphachar + "<span class='count_pp'>" + charAppered.length + "</span>",
      "data-filter": alphachar.toLowerCase(),
      "class": (charAppered.length <= 0) ? "disabled" : ""
    }).appendTo(filterUl);
  }
  filterUl.appendTo($(".filtersection"));
  $("body").on("click", ".filtersection ul li", function() {
    var dis = $(this),
      disFilter = dis.attr("data-filter") || "";
    if (!dis.hasClass("disabled")) {
      dis.addClass("current").siblings("li").removeClass("current");
      if (disFilter != "" && disFilter != "*")
        $(".alpha-filter").hide().filter(function() {
          return $(this).text().trim().charAt(0).toLowerCase() == disFilter.toLowerCase()
        }).show();
      else
        $(".alpha-filter").show();
    }
  });

 var slider = $('#slider-thumb .filter-by-section-description-wrapper').bxSlider({
      "mode": "fade",
      "auto": true,
      "pager": false,
      "speed": 1000,
      "pause": 9000,
      "controls": false,
      "onSlideBefore": function($slideElement, oldIndex, newIndex) {
        $("#slider-thumb .filter-by-section .dTab li[data-slide-index='" + newIndex + "']").addClass("active").siblings("li").removeClass("active");
      }
    });

$("#slider-thumb .filter-by-section .dTab li").click(function() {
      slider.goToSlide($(this).attr("data-slide-index"));
      $(this).addClass("active").siblings("li").removeClass("active");
      slider.stopAuto();
    });

$('.homeslider').bxSlider({
      controls: false,
          auto: true,
          easing: 'ease-in',
          pager: ($(".homeslider > li").length > 1) ? true : false,
          pause: 7000,
          speed: 1000,
          mode: 'fade',
          responsive: true,
          adaptiveHeight: true,
          touchEnabled: false
    });      
$('.bx-pager-item').mouseenter(function(){
        homeSlider.stopAuto();     
      });
      $('.bx-pager-item').mouseleave(function(){
        homeSlider.startAuto();        
      });

function initTab(selc,tSelc,attr,fPrefix,callback) {
      $(selc).click(function(){
        var dis = $(this),
          disTarget = dis.attr(attr||"data-target");
        dis.addClass("active").siblings().removeClass("active");
        $(tSelc).removeClass("active").filter((fPrefix||"")+disTarget).addClass("active");
        (typeof(callback) == "function")&&callback(disTarget);
      }).eq(0).trigger("click");
    }
initTab(".tab-list-warp ul li",".each-team",null,"#",null)

function isRealDevice() {
      return /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|macintosh|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent) && (typeof(window.orientation) != "undefined" || (navigator.maxTouchPoints > 1));
    }
var homeSlider = "";
    function homeSliderInit() {
      $('.slider-wrap').removeClass("loading").find("#loader").remove();
      $('.slider-wrap')
      if (homeSlider == "") {
        homeSlider = $('.slider-wrap').owlCarousel({
          loop: true,
          margin: 0,
          nav: true,
          items: 1,
          dots: true,
          autoplay: true,
          animateOut: 'fadeOut',
        });
      } 
    }
    $(".slider-wrap").imagesLoaded(homeSliderInit);
 //Window Reinit on resize
    function reInitSliderOnResize() {
      homeSliderInit();
    }
    var prop_resize_time = "",
    wRevent = isRealDevice() ? "orientationchange" : "resize";
    $(window).on(wRevent, function() {
      clearTimeout(prop_resize_time);
      prop_resize_time = setTimeout(reInitSliderOnResize, 200);
    });

  <div id="utm_source_hidden_checkout_field">

  </div>
  <div id="utm_content_hidden_checkout_field">
    <input type="hidden" class="input-hidden" name="utm_content" id="utm_content" value="">
  </div>
  <div id="utm_campaign_hidden_checkout_field">
    <input type="hidden" class="input-hidden" name="utm_campaign" id="utm_campaign" value="">
  </div>
  <div id="utm_medium_hidden_checkout_field">
    <input type="hidden" class="input-hidden" name="utm_medium" id="utm_medium" value="">
  </div>
  <div id="utm_term_hidden_checkout_field">
    <input type="hidden" class="input-hidden" name="utm_term" id="utm_term" value="">
  </div>
  <div id="xuid_hidden_checkout_field">
    <input type="hidden" class="input-hidden" name="xuid" id="xuid" value="">
  </div>













$(document).ready(function() {
   var utm_source = Cookies.get('utm_source');
   var utm_content = Cookies.get('utm_content');
   var utm_campaign = Cookies.get('utm_campaign');
   var utm_medium = Cookies.get('utm_medium');
   var utm_term = Cookies.get('utm_term');
   var xuid = Cookies.get('xuid');

   $("#utm_source_hidden_checkout_field").val(utm_source);
   $("#utm_content_hidden_checkout_field").val(utm_content);
   $("#utm_campaign_hidden_checkout_field").val(utm_campaign);
   $("#utm_medium_hidden_checkout_field").val(utm_medium);
   $("#utm_term_hidden_checkout_field").val(utm_term);
   $("#xuid_hidden_checkout_field").val(xuid);
});

}







$(".open").on("click", function(){
  $(".overlay, .modal").addClass("active");
});
$(".close, .overlay").on("click", function(){
   $(".overlay, .modal").removeClass("active");
});
$(document).keyup(function(e) {
  if (e.keyCode === 27) {
    $(".overlay, .modal").removeClass("active");
  }
});

$("a[href^='#']").click(function(e) {
  e.preventDefault();
  var position = $($(this).attr("href")).offset().top;
  $("body, html").animate({
    scrollTop: position
  } /* speed */ );
});

50. On Focus Highlight Label

  • Styling
  • Script
  • Result

  <label for="firstname">First Name</label>
  <input id="firstname" type="text"><br><br>
  <label for="lastname">Last Name</label>
  <input id="lastname" type="text"><br><br>
  <label for="age">Age</label>
  <input id="age" type="text"><br><br>

  <input id="address" type="text">

  .labelfocus {
    color: red;
  }






$(document).ready(function() {
  $("form :input").focus(function() {
  $("label[for='" + this.id + "']").addClass("labelfocus");
  }).blur(function() {
  $("label").removeClass("labelfocus");
  });
});

  #content span {

  }

    width: 900px;
    margin: 0 auto;

$(document).ready(function(){
$("img").hide();
var speed = 200; //speed in ms

$(window).on('load', function() {
$("#content img").hide();
timer= setInterval(function(){
$notLoaded = $("#content img").not(".loaded");
$notLoaded.eq(Math.floor(Math.random()*$notLoaded.length))
.fadeIn()
.addClass("loaded");
if ($notLoaded.length == 0) {
clearInterval(timer);
}
}
, speed);

});

});
